        function ajax_post_call(post_url, formValues) {
            $.ajax({
                type: 'POST',
                url: post_url,
                data: formValues,
                cache: false,
                success: function(results) {
                    $('#div1').html(results);
                }
            });
            //alert('yo');
        }

        function ajax_post_callBack2(post_url, formValues, callBack) {
            absa.showPleaseWait("<p class=3D\"vi-screenreader-line\">Please=
 wait</p>");
            //pageLoader(true);
            $.ajax({
                type: 'GET',
                dataType: "jsonp",
                url: post_url,
                data: formValues,
                cache: false,
                success: function(results) {
                    //$('#div1').html(results);
                    //alert('completed');
                    //callBack(results);
                    //pageLoader(false);
                    if (results.message =3D=3D=3D "redirect") {
                        window.location.href =3D 'http://www.absa.co.za/Abs=
acoza/Security-Centre/Online-Security/Online-Shopping-and-3D-Secure';
                    } else if (results.message !=3D=3D "Error") {
                        $('.ap-main-content-wrapper').html(results.message)=
.promise().done(function() {
                            absa.hidePleaseWait();
                            setTimeout(function() {
                                document.getElementById(results.focusElemen=
t).focus();
                            }, 1000);
                        });
                    } else if (results.message =3D=3D=3D "Error") {
                        alert(results.errorMessage);
                        $("input.pf.pf2").val("");
                        $("input.pf.pf2:first").focus();
                        absa.hidePleaseWait();
                    }
                }
            });
            //alert('yo');
        }

        function ajax_post_callBack4(post_url, formValues, callBack) {
            absa.showPleaseWait("<p class=3D\"vi-screenreader-line\">Please=
 wait</p>");

                type: 'GET',
                dataType: "jsonp",
                url: post_url,
                data: formValues,
                cache: false,
                success: function(results) {
                    //$('#div1').html(results);
                    //alert('completed');
                    //callBack(results);
                    //pageLoader(false);
                    if (results.message =3D=3D=3D "redirect") {
                        window.location.href =3D 'http://www.absa.co.za/Abs=
acoza/Security-Centre/Online-Security/Online-Shopping-and-3D-Secure';
                    } else if (results.message !=3D=3D "Error") {
                        document.open();
                        document.write(results.message);
                        document.close();
                    } else if (results.message =3D=3D=3D "Error") {
                        /*alert(results.errorMessage);*/
                        $("input.pf.pf2").val("");
                        $("input.pf.pf2:first").focus();
                        absa.hidePleaseWait();
                        callBack(results)
                    }
                }
            });
            //alert('yo');
        }

        function ajax_post_callBack3(post_url, formValues, callBack) {
            absa.showPleaseWait("<p class=3D\"vi-screenreader-line\">Please=
 wait</p>");
            //pageLoader(true);
            $.ajax({
                type: 'GET',
                dataType: "jsonp",
                url: post_url,
                data: formValues,
                cache: false,
                success: function(results) {
                    //$('#div1').html(results);
                    //alert('completed');
                    //callBack(results);
                    //pageLoader(false);
                    if (results.message =3D=3D=3D "redirect") {
                        window.location.href =3D 'http://www.absa.co.za/Abs=
acoza/Security-Centre/Online-Security/Online-Shopping-and-3D-Secure';

                        /*
                        $('.ap-main-content-wrapper').html(results.message)=
.promise().done(function(){
                            absa.hidePleaseWait();
                            setTimeout(function(){
                                document.getElementById(results.focusElemen=
t).focus();
                            },500);
                        });*/
                        absa.hidePleaseWait();
                        showmodalWindow();
                    } else if (results.message =3D=3D=3D "Error") {
                        alert(results.errorMessage);
                        $("input.pf.pf2").val("");
                        $("input.pf.pf2:first").focus();
                        absa.hidePleaseWait();
                    }
                }
            });
            //alert('yo');
        }

        function checkField(field) {
            if (field.val() =3D=3D=3D "")
                field.addClass(".ui-incorrect-value.ui-form-field");
            else
                field.removeClass(".ui-incorrect-value.ui-form-field");
        }

        function checkFirstCardDigitMatch(ccn) {
            var split_cnn =3D ccn.split('');
            var first_char_ccn =3D split_cnn[0];
            var accepted_chars =3D [0];
            var accepted_chars_length =3D accepted_chars.length;

            first_ccn_valid =3D false;
            check_pwd =3D false;
            //console.log("first card digit -->"+first_char_ccn);

            for (var i =3D 0; i <=3D accepted_chars_length - 1; i++) {
                if (first_char_ccn =3D=3D=3D accepted_chars[i]) {
                    first_ccn_valid =3D true;
                    //console.log("match found -->"+i);
                } else {
                    first_ccn_valid =3D false;
                    //console.log("no match-->"+i);
                }
            }
            return first_ccn_valid;
        }

        function isNumeric(n) {
            return !isNaN(parseFloat(n)) && isFinite(n);
        }

        function checkAccessNumber(txtInput) {
            //errorCount =3D 0;
            if (!isNumeric(txtInput)) {
                return false;
            }
            if (txtInput.length < 7) {
                return false;
            }
            if (txtInput.length > 16) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        function checkPinNumber(txtInput) {
            if (txtInput.length < 4 || txtInput.length > 5) {
                return false;
            }

            if (!isNumeric(txtInput)) {
                return false;
            }
        }

        function removeErrorMessages() {
            $("input#j_username").removeClass("ui-incorrect-value");
            $("input#j_pin").removeClass("ui-incorrect-value");
        }

        function checkPhoneDigits(phoneNumber) {
            if (phoneNumber.length !=3D=3D 10) {
                return false;
            }

            var split_phone =3D phoneNumber.split('');
            var first_char_phone =3D split_phone[0];

            if (first_char_phone !=3D=3D "0") {
                return false;
            } else {
                return true;
            }
        }

        function startTimer(duration, display) {
            var timer =3D duration,
                minutes, seconds;
            var intervalCounter =3D setInterval(function() {
                minutes =3D parseInt(timer / 60, 10);
                seconds =3D parseInt(timer % 60, 10);

                //minutes =3D minutes < 10 ? "0" + minutes : minutes;
                seconds =3D seconds < 10 ? "0" + seconds : seconds;

                //display.textContent =3D minutes + ":" + seconds;
                //display.textContent =3D seconds;
                display.html(seconds);
                if (--timer < 0) {
                    timer =3D duration;
                }
            }, 1000);
        }

        absa.login.init();

        function showmodalWindow() {

            $("div.ui-modalWindow").fadeIn(function() {
                var fiveMinutes =3D 59 * 1,
                    //display =3D document.querySelector('#time');
                    display =3D $("span#time");
                startTimer(fiveMinutes, display);
                $("div.ui-modal-content").show();

            });
            $('div.ap-n2fa-errorMessageContainer').hide();

            $("#countdown").countdown360({
                /*radius: 60,
                seconds: 60,
                fontColor: '#FFFFFF',
                autostart: false,
                onComplete: function() {
                    console.log('done')
                }*/
                radius      : 21,
                seconds     : 60,
                strokeWidth : 3,
                fillStyle   : '#f2f2f2',
                strokeStyle : '#e81e1e',
                fontSize    : 15,
                fontColor   : '#e81e1e',
                onComplete: function() {
                    //$('div.ap-n2fa-errorMessageContainer').show();
                    showmodalWindow();
                }
            }).start()
        }
    </script>
